msg:After twelve years, I stepped into Guangxi Zhuang Autonomous Region again. After discussing with my family and making a strategy, we all agreed to travel to Guilin, which is the best in the world. I took the high-speed rail from Zhangjiajie, Hunan for nearly five hours and finally arrived in Guilin North. After a day of playing and eating Guilin's famous vinegar blood duck, my wife suggested going to Yangshuo, a place where the landscape is fake Guilin. There are many hotels in Yangshuo. My wife looked at many different types of hotels. Finally, I chose Shixi Tianyue Hotel because of the reviews.
Environment: The hotel looks very high-end. Each room has a small balcony. There are many public areas with five-star facilities and facilities. There are many green plants and fresh bamboo forests in the swimming pool, children's playground, tea room, and public areas. There is an urge to take pictures. In addition, standing on the balcony, you can see the panoramic night view of Yangshuo Lijiang River, which is perfect. It is less than ten minutes away from Liu Sanjie Grand Stage. The hotel front desk does not recommend the Lijiang River package, which is perfect.
Room environment: The room is clean and tidy as a whole, without any musty smell. The room ventilation system is very transparent. The toilet and bathroom are larger than many hotels and the bathroom supplies are very high-end.
Bedding: The mattress is comfortable to sit on, not too soft or too hard, and it is very moderate. The pillow is very soft when lying on it. I am a snorer. My wife rarely hears my snoring that night and wants to take the pillow away. The bed is just right for a family of three to sleep on. I like the carefully selected bedding for the merchant.
Equipment: Each room has independent air conditioning, electric curtains, and independent hair dryers.
Bath products: Each bath product is packaged in an independent small bottle and is very delicate.
Light: North-south transparency, open the balcony door, white curtains flutter in the wind, and the sun shines in, which is very beautiful.
Breakfast: The breakfast is very rich, and occasionally it is not enough, you can tell the waiter to add it.
Tips: Ask to go early in the afternoon when playing in West Street to avoid the crowds and it is not very crowded. The hotel is really comfortable to live in. The family of three all like the hotel. I hope the hotel business will get better and better.

The girl was very enthusiastic and told me that the pier was not far from the hotel and was next to the West Street. If there were not a lot of luggage, I could experience the West Street during the day first. If there were a lot of luggage, the hotel would provide a paid shuttle service. Just tell the hotel front desk in advance. I personally think it's nothing. It's normal to charge a reasonable fee for comfortable service.
It was always rainy and sunny during the stay. It was also very convenient to go out for dinner. There were many restaurants around, most of which were beer fish. We chose Liu Jie's beer fish, which felt pretty good.
It was almost eleven thirty when I returned to the hotel after shopping in the evening. I was tired and afraid of being thirsty at night. I always had to drink water at night. There were two bottles in the room and I felt it was not enough, so I called the front desk to try and see if I could get two more bottles of water. They agreed very readily and delivered them to the room quickly. I checked out at noon and had to take a bus to Guilin, so I asked for two more bottles, which was also no problem. I think this is very good and can meet the needs of guests.
The scenery of the hotel is also very good. The Sky City is beautiful. It's a pity that it's raining so I can't take pictures. The water of the Li River is yellow and I can't experience the clear bottom. In short, the experience is very good. Everyone I met in the hotel is very polite and friendly. The two girls at the front desk are very enthusiastic and treat everyone warmly. Next time I will choose a time to see the clear bottom view and stay here again.

msg:In fact, I really want to recommend this hotel. Among domestic private hotels of the same level and in such a small town, this one is actually very good. If it weren't for the smell of sewerage in the lower floor bathroom and the town's electricity problem, which caused the power to go out in the middle of the night for two nights.

Its advantages: The entire hotel is neat and clean because it is new, and the environment is comfortable. The service attitude is very good, which is very important. If we ask for anything, the waiters will respond quickly and positively. Even the cleaning lady will greet us warmly when she sees us, which is comparable to many star brand hotels. The breakfast is also very good, clean and hygienic, and the variety is good. The layout of the room and the supplies inside are not cheap, and they are all provided. Before departure, we were worried that the facilities were not complete. This was beyond our expectations before moving in. There is a small open-air viewing garden on the 9th floor of the hotel, which is quite comfortable. The picture below was taken in the garden.
      When I checked out, I happened to meet someone from the hotel who was probably the person in charge. He explained to me the reason for the power outage very seriously and even gave me a small apology gift. It can be seen that the mentality of this hotel from top to bottom still wants to do a good job in the hotel. However, they are powerless and helpless due to the impact of urban power facilities. If this can be solved, I personally really like this hotel.

       In addition to the electricity problem, another reason may be that the floor is low. There is a smell coming from the sewer. I wonder if guests who have stayed on the lower floor have had the same problem before. We originally booked a suite with a living room, but got the suite on the 3rd floor on the first day we arrived. We had a great first night. The two guest rooms have a large living room that is separated from each other without affecting each other. The living room and the room are large enough, and the most important thing is that the rooms have their own bathrooms, which is great. It started to rain lightly the next day. We went out to play. When we came back in the afternoon, we found that the bathroom in the master bedroom had a smell. Moreover, the bathroom in this room type has no door, so the smell made it impossible to sleep. Later, the front desk upgraded us to a two-story duplex room on the 7th floor, which was no problem, and they also gave us a fruit plate. This suite is also very good. It has a large balcony, a large room, and snacks. There are also separate bathrooms on the upper and lower floors. I wonder if this low-rise smell problem can be solved by the hotel, or is it a hidden danger left during the infrastructure construction? If this is solved and the electricity problem is taken care of, then this hotel with such configuration and design and such services will be quite good among domestic hotels of the same level. It is not easy to survive in the current economic environment. Personally, I still hope that it can continue to get better and better.

msg:As a family who likes to travel, our requirements for hotel accommodation are higher than for food. After searching, checking, and comparing the working hours of the two days, this time I wanted to stay in a better hotel in Yangshuo town, but I felt that Shixi was better in comparison.
Room: The window faces the Li River, the scenery is good, and the Guilin landscape has her unique beauty! The room facilities are very good, there are wireless charging facilities, and the mobile phone can be charged as soon as it is placed. give it a like! The color of the room, the color and style of the sofa, etc., it can be seen that the management or the owner of the hotel is quite attentive.
Location: Opposite the hotel is the Lijiang River. We can get a bird's-eye view of the Lijiang River from the garden on the top floor, as well as the scenery of a bridge. Visually, it should be the best viewing area in the county.
Breakfast: The breakfast is in the form of a set meal, including Guilin rice noodles, eggs, fruit, milk, dumplings, sweet potatoes. There are many varieties and a lot of weight.
Service: The service is not bad, there is a self-service laundry room, which is quite convenient. There are also swimming pools and children's playgrounds, which are still large-scale playgrounds. If you bring the children with you next time, you should like them very much!

The elderly live on the first floor. Our couple and our children live on the second floor. It is very convenient to take care of them together. The room has a lot of space. You can see the Lijiang River from the floor-to-ceiling windows in the room. The second floor of the duplex has a large balcony, which is very nice. In this way, it is very convenient to take the children in and take a bath, and rest assured! In the evening, you can walk to West Street in a few minutes. The real one is a hotel that is close to West Street and able to watch the scenery while lying in bed.
